 kaha jaataa he ki navaratri main rangon kaa bhi vishesh mahatv hota he
 This time, in worship of the nine forms of Maa Durga, wear special colored clothes and worship Maa Durga
 nau dinon main nau rangon ke kapade pahanane or maa kii puja karne kaa khaas mahatv he
 Each color has a special effect on you
 aapako pataa hi hoga ki kuch log rang-chikitsa yani color-therapy bhi kar rahe hai
 They use bottles of different colors for treatment, because the colors have a special effect on you
 navaratri ke nau dinon ke dauraan kaale rang ke kapade pahananaa varjit hota he
 Therefore, do not wear dark colored clothes
 (navratri First day Color) navaratri ke pehle din kaa rang-pehle din maa shailaputree or maa brahraachaarini kii puja hogi
 Wearing yellow color will be especially auspicious in this puja
 pehla din buudhvaar he isliye hare rang kaa kapadaa bhi pahan sakate hai
 (navratri Second day Color) The color of the second day of Navratri - Mother Chandraghanta will be worshiped on the second day of Navratri
 is din aap grey rang ke kapade pahan kar maa durga ko khush kar sakate hai

 is din aap naarangi rang ko pahan sakate he
 Mother Kushmanda likes orange color
 (navratri Fourth day Color) navaratri ke chauthe din kaa rang-navaratri ke chauthe din skandamata puja kii jaaegi
 Wearing white on this day is considered auspicious
 (navratri Fifth day Color) navaratri ke paanchave din kaa rang-navaratri ke 5wein din maa saraswati kii puja kii jaaegi
 Wearing white or yellow color is considered auspicious on this day
 (navratri Sixth day Color) navaratri ke 6wein din kaa rang-navaratri ke chhathen din maa katyayani kii puja kii jaati he

 ugte suraj kaa rang bhi laal hota he

 josh or ullas kaa rang laal hi he

 This does not mean that the two have any relationship
 bich main bhi kai anya kaaran hote hai
 The currencies of other countries have an impact but sometimes the Indian rupee is weak even when the currencies of other countries are getting stronger
 live mint par 17 disambar 2014 kaa ek lekh dekh rahaa tha
 The Indian rupee was then at a 13-month low
 dollar ke mukaable
 At that time, South Korea's currency won were getting stronger
 japaana kaa yen bhi 1
 17 percent was also strengthened
 singapore kaa dollar, malaysia kaa ringet bhi majboot hua tha
 The currency crisis was disintegrating due to the crisis of the European Union in 2011 and the financial crisis in Greece in 2012 affected the currencies of the world
 28 agast 2013 ko jab bharat kaa rupaya ek dollar ke mukaable 68 par pahunchaa tha tab ek pramukh kaaran temper tentaram bhi tha
 To reinvigorate the US economy, the Federal Reserve increased the dollar and said that the Fed would no longer buy the Reserve Bond
 iskaa asar duniya bhar kii bazaaron or karency par padaa tha
 This is called the taper tantrum
 kabhi duniya ke bazaar main kachche tel kaa daam badhata he to karency kamazor hone lagati he
 This time it has declined due to turkey
 bas raajnneeti ko chunanaa hota he ki use kab in tarkon ko kinare kar apni dukaan chalaani hoti he
 Lies have to be told
 aap jaanate hai ki is vakt america or china ke bich vyapaarik yuddh chal rahaa he
 Both countries increase taxes on each other's imports
 is vakt america kii arthvyavastha majboot sthiti main he is kaaran bhi duniya bhar dollar kaa pravaah america kii taraf ho rahaa he
 American investors are withdrawing money from other markets and investing in their markets
 is majbooti kaa laabh uthaakar trump ne china ke khilaaf morcha khol diya he
 China is also increasing the import duty on goods imported from America
 iskaa asar duusare mulkon par bhi pad rahaa he
 The United States has clashed against many countries including China, Iran, Turkey, India simultaneously
 bharat ne bhi kai amareeki chizon par aayaat shulk badha diya he
 An Angle America and Turkey are at loggerheads
 america ne turki se steel or alumunium kaa aayaat shulk 20 pratishat se badhaakar 50 pratishat kar diya he
 This will reduce the demand for turkey steel
 isse gussa hokar turki ke raashtrapati erdogan ne kaha he ki unka desh amareeki electronics kaa bahishkaar karegaa
 Looking at their stand, speculations are being made as to whether they will really do this or just say at the level of threat
 erdogan ne kaha he ki ham jo bhi america se mangate hai usase behatar apane desh main bana lenge
 If they have an iphone, then so is Samsung
 hamaare desh main venus he
 These are all brands of phones
 yah abhi saaf nahi he ki argodan ise aupchaarik rup denge yaa abhi maamla dhamkee tak hi simit he
 The turkey lira weakened 25 percent in this trade war last month
 tippaniyan In 2016 cyber hackers hacked the Central Bank of Bangladesh and pulled out $ 101 million
 isamen se 20 milayan dollar srilanka ke haikaron ke paas gaya tha, jise waapas hasil kar liya gaya
 $ 81 million was gone to the Philippines, of which $ 18 million was returned
 iske aage kii jaankaree nahin he magar ye isliye bataa rahaa hum ki bharat main bhi is tarah kaa prayaas hua he
 The hackers have flown 94 crores from a co-operative bank in Pune
 hamaare sahyogi sunil singh ne report bheji he ki bharat sahit 29 deshon main debit card ke zarie paise nikaale gaye hai
 Never before has there been such a huge cyber robbery in India
 11 agast ko bank ke sweaching system ko hack kar 7 ghante ke bheetar 28 deshon main 12 hazaar baar tranjection hua or 78 karod nikaal liye gaye
 There were 2849 transactions within India and two and a half crores were withdrawn
 phir 13 agast ko 14 karod or uda liye
 Kasamas Bank has shut down its payment system for two days but has comforted customers that their money is safe
 chintaa na karen
 The bank has registered an FIR
 kya rupee ke kamazor hone main sarkaar kaa role hota he? nahin
 Then why doesn't the government say this to itself
 is uttar sarkaar hi de sakati he magar aap ges kar sakate hai ki sarkaar kyon nahin kahati he ki rupaya uske kaaran kamazor nahin hua he
 Because as soon as she says this, people will ask how she used to say that the rupee was weakening due to the policies of the UPA government
 hamane praanjay guha thakurta se poocha he ki kya ve un kaarnon ko bataa sakate hai jiske kaaran rupaya kamazor hota he
 Government does not play a role
 bhartiya reserve bank kaa hota he
 If he wants to sell the dollar, increase its supply in the market and stop the rupee from falling
 dollar ke mukaable rupaya kamazor hone se sabase adhik asar petrol deazal ke daam par padataa he
 Petrol prices start rising
 saath hi baahar se chizon kaa aayaat mahangaa hone lagata he
 If the rupee is weak then the foreign investor will get less returns
 baharhaal rupee kii raajnneeti se sarkaar ne kinaaraa kar liya he
 The opposition has embraced him
 vaise bijepi ke pravaktaa nalin kohli ne jo kaha he wo kaam kii baat kahi he
 He has said that those who read newspapers know why all this is happening
 bharat ke aarthik maamalon ke sachiv subhash chander garg ne riter se kaha he ki ise lekar chintaa karne kii koi zarurat nahin he kyoki rupee main yah giravat bahari factor ke kaaran aa rahi he
 The currency of other economies is also weakening
 is str par reserve bank ke dollar bech kar giravat ko rokane kii koshish kaa khaas phayda nahin hoga
 Even if the rupee falls to 80, it will not be a matter of concern
 barshate duusari karency bhi kamazor hoti rahi
 Where was the India where the country's independence was in danger when it became 68 rupees, today the Secretary of Economic Affairs says that even a dollar will be 80 rupees, even if there is no worry, the currency of other countries will also be weak 
 yaa to tark badal gaya he yaa vaaki zamana badal gaya he
 So will it be 80 rupees? kya 2013 ke pehle sirf bhartiya rupaya gir rahaa tha, anya deshon kii karency main giravat nahin aa rahi thi
 Exactly the same was happening at that time
 live mint ke ek lekh ke anusaar is vakt bhartiya rupee ke alaava turki ke lira main sabase adhik giravat darj hui he

 is kaaran euro kaa bhav bhi dollar ke mukaable kamazor hue he

 china bhi america se aaayaatit chizon par aayaat shulk badhaate ja rahaa he
 This is having an impact on other countries as well
 america ek saath china, iran, turki, bharat sahit kai deshon ke khilaaf bhida hua he
 India has also increased import duties on many American items
 ek angel america or turki aapas main bhide hue hai

 isse hoga yah ki turki ke steel kii maang kam ho jaaegi

 1784 AD kaa pits india act:is act ke dwaara dohare prashasan kaa prarambh hua-(i) court of diarectors - vyapaarik maamalon ke liye(ii) board of controlar- raajnneetik maamalon ke liye
 3
 1793 i
 Charter Act of: It provided for the payment of salaries, etc
 of the members of the Board of Control, out of Indian revenue
 4
 1813 AD kaa charter adhinium:iske dwaara(i)company ke adhikaar-patr ko 20 saalon ke liye badha diya gaya
 (ii) The company's monopoly on trade with India was taken away
 lekin use china ke saath vyaper or purvi deshon ke saath chaay ke vyapaar ke sambandh main 20 saalon ke liye ekadhikaar praapt rahaa
 (iii) Trade with India opened to all British citizens subject to certain limitations
 5
 1833 AD kaa charter adhinium:iske dwaara(i)company ke vyapaarik adhikaar purnatah samaapt kar die gaye
 (ii) Now, the task of the company is to rule India only on behalf of the British government
 (iii)bengalag ke governor jaranal ko bharat kaa governor general kaha jane laga
 (iv) Indian laws were classified and arrangements were made for the appointment of Law Commission for this work
 6
 1853 AD
 kaa charter adhinium:is adhinium ke dwaara sevaaon main naamajadagi kaa siddhant samaapt kar company ke mahatvapurn padon ko pratiyogi parikshaon ke aadhaar par bharne kii vyavastha kii gai
 7
 1858 i
 Charter Act of: (i) The rule of India was handed over from the company to the British Crown
 (ii)bharat main mantri-pad kii vyavastha kii gai
 (iii) India Council of 15 members was created
 (iv)bhartiya maamalon par british sansad kaa sidhaa niyantran sthapit kiya gaya
 8
 1861 i
 Government of India Act: The Governor General's Executive Council was expanded, (ii) the departmental system was introduced, (iii) the Governor General was empowered to issue ordinances for the first time
 (iv)governor jaranal ko bengal, uttar-pashchimi seemaa praant or punjab main vidhaan parishad sthapit karne kii shakti pradaan kii gai
 9
 1892 i
 Government of India Act: (i) Indirect Election System was introduced, (ii) It gave power to debate revenue and expenditure or budget and to ask questions to the executive
 10
 The Government of India Act of 1909 [marley-minto Reform] - (i) Provision of separate representation for Muslim community for the first time
 (ii)bharatiyon ko bharat sachiv evam governor general kii kaaryakarini parishadon main niyukti kii gai
 (iii) The Central and Provincial Legislative Councils were empowered to debate the budget for the first time, to propose proposals on subjects of public interest, to ask supplementary questions and to vote
 (iv) prantiy vidhaan parishadon kii sankhya main vruddhi kii gai
 11
 1919 i0 kaa bharat shashan adhinium [maantegue chamsford sudhaar] -(i)centre main dwisadanaatmak vidhayika kii sthapana kii gai- pratham rajya parishad tathaa duusari kendriya vidhaan sabha
 The number of members of the Council of State was 60; In which 34 were elected and their tenure was for 5 years
 kendriya vidhaan sabha ke sadasyon kii sankhya 145 thi, jinamein 104 niwarchit tathaa 41 manonith hote the
 His tenure was 3 years
 donon sadanon ke adhikaar samaan the
 The only difference was that the lower house had the authority to approve the budget
 (ii)praanto main dwaidh shashan pranali kaa pravartan kiya gaya
 According to this plan, the provincial subjects were divided into two subclasses - reserved and transferred
 arakshit vishay the - vitt, bhoomikar, akaal sahaayta, nyaay, police, pension, aapraadhik jatiyaan, chhapaakhana, samachar patr, sinchai, jalmaarg, khan, kaarkaana, bijli, gas, vyallar, shramik kalyaan, aughogic vivaad, motargadiyaan, chote bandargah or saarvajanik sevaayen aadi
 Subjects transferred - (i) Education, library, museum, local autonomous governance, medical aid
 (ii)saarvajanik nirmaan vibhaag, aabkaari, ughog, taul tathaa maap, saarvajanik manoranjan par niyantran, dharmik tathaa agrahar daan aadi
 (iii) The Governor administers the reserved subject through his Executive Council; Whereas the transferred subject was administered by the Indian Ministers responsible to the Provincial Legislature
 (iv)dwaidh shashan pranali ko 1935 i0 ke act ke dwaara samaapt kar diya gaya
 (v) The Secretary of India was empowered to appoint the Auditor General of India
 (vi)is adhinium ne bharat main ek lok seva ayog ke gathan kaa praavdhaan kiya
 12
 1935 i0 kaa bharat shashan adhinium: 1935 i0 ke adhinium main 451 dharaaen or 15 parishisht the
 The salient features of the Act are as follows: (i) All India Union: This union was to be made up of 11 British provinces, 6 Chief Commissioner's territories and native princely states who voluntarily joined the Union
 praanton ke liye sangh main sammilit hona anivaary tha, kintu deshi riyasaton ke liy yah echhik tha
 The princely states did not join the union and there was no opportunity to issue a declaration regarding the establishment of the proposed union
 (ii)prantiy swytta: is adhinium ke dwaara praanto main dwaidh shashan vyavastha kaa ant kar unhen ek swatantra or swashasit sanvaidhanik aadhaar pradaan kiya gaya
 (iii) Establishment of diarchy at the center: Some federal subjects [security, foreign relations, religious matters] were kept in the hands of the Governor General
 anya sangheey vishyon kii vyavastha ke liye governor- general ko sahaayta evam paraamarsh dene hetu mantrimandal kii vyavastha kii gai, jo mantrimandal vyavasthapika ke prati uttaradaayi tha
 (iv) Arrangement of Federal Court: Its jurisdiction extended to the provinces and princely states
 is nyaayalay main ek mukhya nyaayadhish tathaa do anya nyaayadhishon kii vyavastha kii gai
 The ultimate power of the court was vested with the Privy Council [london]
 (v) british sansad kii sarvocchata:is adhinium main kisi bhi prakaar ke parivartan kaa adhikaar british sansad ke paas tha
 Provincial Legislature and Federal Administrator: There was no change in this
 (vi)bharat parishad kaa ant :is adhinium ke dwaara bharat parishad kaa ant kar diya gaya
 (vii) Expansion of communal electoral system: The communal electoral system was continued to represent various sects in the federal and provincial administrations and was also extended to Anglo Indians - Indian Christians, Europeans and Harijans
 (viii)is adhinium main prastaavna kaa abhaav tha
 (xi) By this Burma was separated from India, Aden was subjugated to the colonial office of England and Berar was incorporated into the Central Province
 13
 Indian Independence Act of 1947: Indian Independence Act was proposed in the British Parliament on 4 July 1947, which was approved on 18 July 1947
 is adhinium main 20 dharaaen thim
 The major provisions of the Act are as follows - (i) Establishment of two dominions: On August 15, 1947, two dominions, namely India and Pakistan, will be made, and the British Government will hand over power to them
 satta kaa uttardaayitv donon adhirajyon kii samvidhan sabha ko saunpa jayega
 (ii) There will be one governor-general in each of the India and Pakistan Governments, to be appointed with the advice of his Cabinet
 (iii)samvidhan sabha kaa vidhaan mandal ke rup main kaary karnaa- jab tak samvidhan sabhaayen samvidhan kaa nirmaan nai kar letin, tab tak vah vidhaan mandal ke rup main kaary karti rahengin
 (iv) The posts of Minister of India will be abolished
 (v)1935 i0 ke bhartiya shashan adhinium dwaara shashan jab tak samvidhan sabha dwaara nayaa samvidhan banaakar taiyaar nahin kiya jaataa he; tab tak us samay 1935 i0 ke bhartiya shashan adhinium dwaara hi shashan hoga
 (vi) Britain's supremacy over native princely states was abolished
 unako bharat yaa pakistan kisi bhi adhirajya main sammalit hone or apane bhavi sambandho kaa nishchay karne kii swatantraaa pradaan kii gai

 Sun and lunar eclipse have great importance in Hinduism

 There are also many superstitions about eclipse in India, while science does not accept any superstitions about eclipses

 Let us know when and how the eclipse occurs: Solar eclipse: (1) When the moon comes between the sun and the earth, the bright surface of the sun is not visible due to the moon
 (2)chandramaa kii vajah se jab surya dhakne lagata he to is sthiti ko suryagrahan kehete hai
 (3) When a part of the sun is hidden, it is called partial solar eclipse
 (4)jab surya kuch der ke liye puri tarah se chandramaa ke peeche chhip jaataa he to use purna suryagrahan kehete hai
 (5) Full solar eclipse always occurs on Amavasya
 chandragrahan:(1)jab surya or chandramaa ke bich prithvi aa jaati he to surya kii puri roshni chandramaa par nahin padati he
 This is called lunar eclipse
 (2)jab surya, prithvi or chandramaa ek saral rekha main hote hai to chandragrahan kii sthiti hoti he
 (3) The lunar eclipse always occurs on the full moon night
 (4)ek saal main adhiktam teen baar prithvi ke upachaaya se chandramaa gujarata he, tabhi chandragrahan lagata he
 (5) Like solar eclipse, lunar eclipse can be partial and complete

 bjp's work has increased in every section of the society, Dalit, Adivasi
 hamane kisi varg ko choda nahin he
 Everyone's development is important
 punjab chunavonmen bijepi or sarkaar main rahane kii vajah se jo anti inakambency hota he, uskaa asar hota he
 Therefore, Punjab did not yield the results we expected
 punjab main loksabhaa ke chunaav main bhi apekshit parinaam nahin aae the
 Shrikant Sharma, BJP leaders are the victory of Brajwasis
 brajraj kii aandhi puure pradesh main chal rahi he
 This is the magic of a successful couple who think for the country
 duusari ore ek or jodi he jo sirf apane parivaar ke liye sinchati he
 The public has understood the difference between the two pairs
 main party kaa vafaadaar sipaahi hum
 i am in charge of a state like Himachal
 party ne chunaav ladane kaa aadesh diya or brajvaasiyon ne agaadh pyaar
 My priority will be development of Braj
 janata kaa ye bharosa yaad rahegaa
 Will always follow the party's order
 nitin gadakari, bijepi netaupi main jis tarah ke nattejey aae hai utane ki ummid hamen bhi nahin thi
 This victory is due to poor welfare schemes of Prime Minister Narendra Modi and his vision Sabka Saath Saath Sabka Vikas
 hamen is tarah kii bhi jaankaree mil rahi he ki teen talaaq par sarkaar ke ruukh ke baad muslim mahilaon ne bhi hamen baari sankhya main vot kiya he
 Today, the situation of the Congress will be like a song in Hindi films "hum to druben sanam tum bhi le le drubenge" and it has become like the poison that will go with, it is sure to sink
 jab mulaayam singh ko ye saath pasand nahin tha to janata ko kaise pasand kar sakati thi
 We have not got as many seats as we expected in Goa, but we are definitely going to form the government with the support of independents and one Goa regional party
 goa main mukhyamantri koun hoga ye bijepi sansadeey dal tay karegaa
 Yogi Aditya Nath, BJP leader Aditya Nath said, the people have completely rejected the sp-congress alliance
 yah upi kii janata kaa aashirwad or bijepi kaaryakartaaon kii mehnat he
 i played the role i was given as an MP
 mim afjal, congress netaupi main communal or cast ejineering kii jeet hui he or yah aane vaale samay ke liye achche sanket nahin hai
 If our weakness is that we take every class along, then it is acceptable to us
 kailash vijayawargeey, bijepi netaupi ke jo nattejey jo saamne aa rahe he usase ye saafe ho gaya he ki pradhanmantri narendra modi ne jo kaam kiya he, janata ne uskaa inaam diya he
 It has been proved that the people of UP do not like akhilesh-rahul, because Akhilesh's father did not like this company, Rahul's mother did not like it together, then how would the public like it
 modi ji kaa jaadu kaa pehle se bhi zyaada he janata ke man main
 This victory is the work of the Prime Minister and the victory of Amit Shah's strategy
 mukhyamantri koun hoga yah vidhayak dal or sansadeey board tay karegaa
 The people of Meenakshi Lekhup have given this majority to the BJP on the work of the Prime Minister
 janata ko ye saath pasand nahin aayaa or kaam nahin karnama bolta he, yah upi kii janata ne bataa diya
 After these results, Akhilesh and Rahul decide their own future
 is jeet kaa shrey pradhanmantri narendra modi or amit shah do logon kii jeet ko jaataa he
 Modi's charisma is going to last for several decades
 rajeev shuklachunaavon main haar-jeet lagi rahati he, isliye ghabaraane kii jarurat nahin
 We kept doing politics of development and bjp did religion, caste religion and vote bank politics
 donon kii ladaai main ham haar gaye
 We will do the politics of development even further, but in UP our organization is very weak at the lower level, we will also try to strengthen it
 haar ke liye rahul gandhi ko jimmedaar tehraana galat he
 Rahul is a national leader, Rahul campaigned in Punjab also, we are winning there
